<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reese_Witherspoon&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Influences">Influences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reese_Witherspoon&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Influences">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Witherspoon has cited actresses like <a href="/wiki/Meryl_Streep" title="Meryl Streep">Meryl Streep</a>, <a href="/wiki/Holly_Hunter" title="Holly Hunter">Holly Hunter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Frances_McDormand" title="Frances McDormand">Frances McDormand</a>, <a href="/wiki/Debra_Winger" title="Debra Winger">Debra Winger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Diane_Ladd" title="Diane Ladd">Diane Ladd</a>, <a href="/wiki/Julia_Roberts" title="Julia Roberts">Julia Roberts</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nicole_Kidman" title="Nicole Kidman">Nicole Kidman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jodie_Foster" title="Jodie Foster">Jodie Foster</a>, <a href="/wiki/Goldie_Hawn" title="Goldie Hawn">Goldie Hawn</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sally_Field" title="Sally Field">Sally Field</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sigourney_Weaver" title="Sigourney Weaver">Sigourney Weaver</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lucille_Ball" title="Lucille Ball">Lucille Ball</a>, <a href="/wiki/Carole_Lombard" title="Carole Lombard">Carole Lombard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Judy_Holliday" title="Judy Holliday">Judy Holliday</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gena_Rowlands" title="Gena Rowlands">Gena Rowlands</a>, and actors like <a href="/wiki/Tom_Hanks" title="Tom Hanks">Tom Hanks</a> and <a href="/wiki/Michael_Keaton" title="Michael Keaton">Michael Keaton</a> as influences in her acting.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-reader.27s_digest_17-2"><a href="#cite_note-reader.27s_digest-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185"><a href="#cite_note-185">[185]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-new_you_186-0"><a href="#cite_note-new_you-186">[186]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187"><a href="#cite_note-187">[187]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188"><a href="#cite_note-188">[188]</a></sup> Her favorite films are <i><a href="/wiki/Splendor_in_the_Grass" title="Splendor in the Grass">Splendor in the Grass</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Overboard_(film)" title="Overboard (film)">Overboard</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-new_you_186-1"><a href="#cite_note-new_you-186">[186]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189"><a href="#cite_note-189">[189]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reese_Witherspoon&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Witherspoon met actor <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Phillippe" title="Ryan Phillippe">Ryan Phillippe</a> at her 21st birthday party in March 1997.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-split_end_190-0"><a href="#cite_note-split_end-190">[190]</a></sup> They became engaged in December 1998<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191"><a href="#cite_note-191">[191]</a></sup> and married near <a href="/wiki/Charleston,_South_Carolina" title="Charleston, South Carolina">Charleston, South Carolina</a>, on June 5, 1999, at Old Wide Awake Plantation.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnn_192-0"><a href="#cite_note-cnn-192">[192]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193"><a href="#cite_note-193">[193]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194"><a href="#cite_note-194">[194]</a></sup> The couple have two children together, daughter, Ava Elizabeth Phillippe (born 1999),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195"><a href="#cite_note-195">[195]</a></sup> and son, Deacon Reese Phillippe (born 2003).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cnn_192-1"><a href="#cite_note-cnn-192">[192]</a></sup> In October 2006, Witherspoon and Phillippe announced that they were separating.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196"><a href="#cite_note-196">[196]</a></sup> The following month Witherspoon filed for divorce, citing irreconcilable differences.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-divorce_fox_news_197-0"><a href="#cite_note-divorce_fox_news-197">[197]</a></sup> In her petition, she sought joint legal and sole physical custody of their children, with full visitation rights for Phillippe.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-divorce_fox_news_197-1"><a href="#cite_note-divorce_fox_news-197">[197]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198"><a href="#cite_note-198">[198]</a></sup> With no <a href="/wiki/Prenuptial_agreement" title="Prenuptial agreement">prenuptial agreement</a>, they would be entitled to half of all assets gained during the marriage under California law—with Witherspoon's being the more significant.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199"><a href="#cite_note-199">[199]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200"><a href="#cite_note-200">[200]</a></sup> Witherspoon requested that the court grant no <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spousal_support" title="Spousal support">spousal support</a> for Phillippe, and he did not contest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-divorce_fox_news_197-2"><a href="#cite_note-divorce_fox_news-197">[197]</a></sup> On May 15, 2007, he filed for joint physical custody of their children and made no motion to block Witherspoon from seeking support from him.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ryan_seek_custody_201-0"><a href="#cite_note-ryan_seek_custody-201">[201]</a></sup> Witherspoon and Phillippe's final divorce documents were granted by the Los Angeles Superior Court on October 5, 2007.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202"><a href="#cite_note-202">[202]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-203"><a href="#cite_note-203">[203]</a></sup></p>
<p>Throughout 2007, there was persistent speculation in the mass media about a romantic relationship between Witherspoon and her <i><a href="/wiki/Rendition_(film)" title="Rendition (film)">Rendition</a></i> co-star <a href="/wiki/Jake_Gyllenhaal" title="Jake Gyllenhaal">Jake Gyllenhaal</a>. After her divorce was finalized in October 2007, they became more open about their relationship, mainly due to the release of paparazzi pictures of them vacationing together in <a href="/wiki/Rome" title="Rome">Rome</a>, Italy. They reportedly broke up in December 2009.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204"><a href="#cite_note-204">[204]</a></sup></p>
<p>In early February 2010, it was reported that Witherspoon had begun dating Jim Toth,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-205"><a href="#cite_note-205">[205]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-206"><a href="#cite_note-206">[206]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-207"><a href="#cite_note-207">[207]</a></sup> a <a href="/wiki/Talent_agent" title="Talent agent">talent agent</a> and co-head of motion picture talent at the <a href="/wiki/Creative_Artists_Agency" title="Creative Artists Agency">Creative Artists Agency</a>, where Witherspoon is a client.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-208"><a href="#cite_note-208">[208]</a></sup> Witherspoon and Toth announced their engagement in December 2010,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-209"><a href="#cite_note-209">[209]</a></sup> and married on March 26, 2011 in <a href="/wiki/Ojai,_California" title="Ojai, California">Ojai, California</a>, at Libbey Ranch,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-210"><a href="#cite_note-210">[210]</a></sup> Witherspoon's country estate (which she since has sold).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-211"><a href="#cite_note-211">[211]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-212"><a href="#cite_note-212">[212]</a></sup> The couple's son, Tennessee James Toth, was born on September 27, 2012.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-213"><a href="#cite_note-213">[213]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Filmography">Filmography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reese_Witherspoon&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Filmography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Accolades">Accolades</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reese_Witherspoon&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Accolades">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Reese_Witherspoon" title="List of awards and nominations received by Reese Witherspoon">List of awards and nominations received by Reese Witherspoon</a></div>
<p>Witherspoon has won numerous awards, including the BAFTA Award and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Academy_Award" title="Academy Award">Academy Award</a> for <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress" title="Academy Award for Best Actress">Best Performance by an Actress in a Leading Role</a> for her performance in <i><a href="/wiki/Walk_the_Line" title="Walk the Line">Walk the Line</a></i> in 2005.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-academy-award-bbc_70-1"><a href="#cite_note-academy-award-bbc-70">[70]</a></sup> In 2015, Witherspoon was nominated for another <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress" title="Academy Award for Best Actress">Best Performance by an Actress in a Leading Role</a> for her performance in <i><a href="/wiki/Wild_(2014_film)" title="Wild (2014 film)">Wild</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-academy-award-2015_214-0"><a href="#cite_note-academy-award-2015-214">[214]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reese_Witherspoon&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: References">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
